/>.com</a></span></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n</b> (<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1177148991">.mw-parser-output .IPA-label-small{font-size:85%}.mw-parser-output .references .IPA-label-small,.mw-parser-output .infobox .IPA-label-small,.mw-parser-output .navbox .IPA-label-small{font-size:100%}</style><span class="IPA-label IPA-label-small">Spanish pronunciation:</span> <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="es-Latn-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Spanish" title="Help:IPA/Spanish">&#91;san<span class="wrap"> </span>se\xce\xb2as\xcb\x88tjan&#93;</a></span> <span class="noprint"><span class="ext-phonos"><span data-nosnippet="" id="ooui-php-1" class="ext-phonos-PhonosButton noexcerpt ext-phonos-PhonosButton-emptylabel oo-ui-widget oo-ui-widget-enabled oo-ui-buttonElement oo-ui-buttonElement-frameless oo-ui-iconElement oo-ui-buttonWidget" data-ooui="{&quot;_&quot;:&quot;mw.Phonos.PhonosButton&quot;,&quot;href&quot;:&quot;\\/\\/upload.wikimedia.org\\/wikipedia\\/commons\\/transcoded\\/a\\/ac\\/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n.ogg\\/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n.ogg.mp3&quot;,&quot;rel&quot;:[&quot;nofollow&quot;],&quot;framed&quot;:false,&quot;icon&quot;:&quot;volumeUp&quot;,&quot;data&quot;:{&quot;ipa&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;text&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;lang&quot;:&quot;en&quot;,&quot;wikibase&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;file&quot;:&quot;San Sebasti\\u00e1n.ogg&quot;},&quot;classes&quot;:[&quot;ext-phonos-PhonosButton&quot;,&quot;noexcerpt&quot;,&quot;ext-phonos-PhonosButton-emptylabel&quot;]}"><a role="button" tabindex="0" href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/a/ac/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n.ogg/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n.ogg.mp3" rel="nofollow" aria-label="Play audio" title="Play audio" class="oo-ui-buttonElement-button"><span class="oo-ui-iconElement-icon oo-ui-icon-volumeUp"></span><span class="oo-ui-labelElement-label"></span><span class="oo-ui-indicatorElement-indicator oo-ui-indicatorElement-noIndicator"></span></a></span><sup class="ext-phonos-attribution noexcerpt navigation-not-searchable"><a href="/wiki/File:San_Sebasti%C3%A1n.ogg" title="File:San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n.ogg">\xe2\x93\x98</a></sup></span></span>, <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1177148991"><span class="IPA-label IPA-label-small">locally</span> <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="und-Latn-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA" title="Help:IPA">&#91;\xcb\x8csa\xc5\x8b<span class="wrap"> </span>se\xce\xb2a\xca\x94\xcb\x88tja\xc5\x8b&#93;</a></span>) is a <a href="/wiki/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n_barrio-pueblo" title="San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n barrio-pueblo">town</a> and <a href="/wiki/Municipalities_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Municipalities of Puerto Rico">municipality</a> of <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a> located in the northwestern region of the island, south of <a href="/wiki/Isabela,_Puerto_Rico" title="Isabela, Puerto Rico">Isabela</a>, <a href="/wiki/Quebradillas,_Puerto_Rico" title="Quebradillas, Puerto Rico">Quebradillas</a> and <a href="/wiki/Camuy,_Puerto_Rico" title="Camuy, Puerto Rico">Camuy</a>; north of <a href="/wiki/Las_Mar%C3%ADas,_Puerto_Rico" title="Las Mar\xc3\xadas, Puerto Rico">Las Mar\xc3\xadas</a>; east of <a href="/wiki/Moca,_Puerto_Rico" title="Moca, Puerto Rico">Moca</a> and <a href="/wiki/A%C3%B1asco,_Puerto_Rico" title="A\xc3\xb1asco, Puerto Rico">A\xc3\xb1asco</a>; and west of <a href="/wiki/Lares,_Puerto_Rico" title="Lares, Puerto Rico">Lares</a>. San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n is spread over twenty-four barrios and <a href="/wiki/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n_barrio-pueblo" title="San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n barrio-pueblo">San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n Pueblo</a> (the downtown area and the administrative center of the city). It is a principal city of the <a href="/wiki/Aguadilla-Isabela-San_Sebasti%C3%A1n_Metropolitan_Statistical_Area" class="mw-redirect" title="Aguadilla-Isabela-San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n Metropolitan Statistical Area">Aguadilla-Isabela-San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n Metropolitan Statistical Area</a>.\n</p>\n<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc" />\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="History">History</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size mw-halign-left" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:1929-02_A%C3%B1o_6,_N%C3%BAm._62_Page_28.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/1929-02_A%C3%B1o_6%2C_N%C3%BAm._62_Page_28.jpg/220px-1929-02_A%C3%B1o_6%2C_N%C3%BAm._62_Page_28.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="304" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/1929-02_A%C3%B1o_6%2C_N%C3%BAm._62_Page_28.jpg/330px-1929-02_A%C3%B1o_6%2C_N%C3%BAm._62_Page_28.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/1929-02_A%C3%B1o_6%2C_N%C3%BAm._62_Page_28.jpg/440px-1929-02_A%C3%B1o_6%2C_N%C3%BAm._62_Page_28.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4900" data-file-height="6762" /></a><figcaption>1929 map of San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n</figcaption></figure>\n<p>The permission to found the town was officially granted in 1752, under the leadship of the founder, Captain <a href="/w/index.php?title=Crist%C3%B3bal_Gonz%C3%A1lez_de_la_Cruz&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Crist\xc3\xb3bal Gonz\xc3\xa1lez de la Cruz (page does not exist)">Crist\xc3\xb3bal Gonz\xc3\xa1lez de la Cruz</a>, who among other residents had an interest in converting some cow farms into an agricultural village. The foundation of the town from the religious aspect, was consummated in December 1762 by Mariano Martin, the island catholic bishop at that time. At the beginning, by 1700, San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n was a conglomerate of a few cow farms, owned by some residents of the Partido de Aguada. Las Vegas was the former plain site of one of the first cow farms located by the Guatemala riverside at the north. Also, another of those cow farms was <b>Pepinito</b> (today\'s <a href="/wiki/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n_barrio-pueblo" title="San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n barrio-pueblo">downtown</a>) that was a prominent hill with a white calcium carbonate face. On the north side of the town it can be seen some of this <i>pepinos</i> (<a href="/wiki/Cucumber" title="Cucumber">cucumbers</a>). These two cow farms gave the town its first name. From these geographical features come the first names of the new village: <b>Las Vegas del Pepino</b> (Cucumber Fields). In 1865 it is documented as <b>San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n de Las Vegas del Pepino</b>.\n</p><p>At the beginning of the 19th century, wealthy Spanish families arrived in El Pepino, fleeing the revolutions of <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">Dominican Republic</a>. Later, by 1850, several families from <a href="/wiki/Catalonia" title="Catalonia">Catalonia</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Basque_Country_(greater_region)" title="Basque Country (greater region)">Basque Country</a> in Spain joined the large number of <i><a href="/wiki/Isle%C3%B1os" title="Isle\xc3\xb1os">isle\xc3\xb1os</a></i> (<a href="/wiki/Canary_Islands" title="Canary Islands">Canary Islanders</a>) that had made El Pepino their home. These people, after taking over the local political power, developed a coffee industry and brought some material progress to the town. <a href="/wiki/Basques" title="Basques">Basques</a> in the municipality, in remembrance of their <a href="/wiki/Basque_Country_(greater_region)" title="Basque Country (greater region)">home region</a> and its religious patron, saw the need of updating old traditions used by the Canary Islanders and started to call the town <i>San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n</i>, and thus got the name formally changed by the central government authority. Nevertheless, the citizens of San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n are popularly called <i>pepinianos</i>.\n</p><p>San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n M\xc3\xa1rtir (Spanish for <a href="/wiki/Saint_Sebastian" title="Saint Sebastian">Saint Sebastian</a> the <a href="/wiki/Martyr" title="Martyr">Martyr</a>) is the <a href="/wiki/Patron_saint" title="Patron saint">patron saint</a> of <a href="/wiki/Archery" title="Archery">archers</a> and was chosen to be the patron saint of the town since its early history, first brought by the immigrants from the Canaries and later confirmed by the Basques, with the town name changed in 1869.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Maria" title="Hurricane Maria">Hurricane Maria</a> on September 20, 2017, triggered numerous landslides in San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n with significant amount of rainfall. The hurricane winds knocked all the power out and the town was left in the dark.<sup id="cite_ref-USGS_Maria_Landslides_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-USGS_Maria_Landslides-2"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-USGS_Maria_Landslides_map_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-USGS_Maria_Landslides_map-3"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>The 40,000 residents of San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n were left without electrical power.<sup id="cite_ref-Wired_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Wired-4"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\nTwo weeks after the hurricane decimated the island, <a href="/wiki/Javier_Jim%C3%A9nez_(mayor)" title="Javier Jim\xc3\xa9nez (mayor)">Javier Jim\xc3\xa9nez</a>, the mayor at the time, noticed that help was not on the way. He decided that San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n would not wait for the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Electric_Power_Authority" title="Puerto Rico Electric Power Authority">AEE</a> brigades to come. He assembled an ad hoc team of volunteers, some who were retired AEE electricians, set safety protocols, and their mandate was to get the electrical power back up and running for the people of San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n. \nFour months after the hurricane, they had restored power to 2,500 homes and continued to do about 60 homes each day.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> A monument honoring the accomplishments of the <i>Pepino Power Authority</i>, as they were quickly named, was erected in <i>Plaza de la Identidad Pepiniana</i> in <a href="/wiki/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n_barrio-pueblo" title="San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n barrio-pueblo">San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n barrio-pueblo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>6<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Geography">Geography</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Geography"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.png" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.png/220px-San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="244" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.png/330px-San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/93/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.png/440px-San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.png 2x" data-file-width="1102" data-file-height="1222" /></a><figcaption>Subdivisions of San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n</figcaption></figure>\n<p>San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n is on the northwest.<sup id="cite_ref-PR_Ency_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PR_Ency-7"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Water_features">Water features</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Water features"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Guajataca_Lake" title="Guajataca Lake">Guajataca Lake</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/R%C3%ADo_Grande_de_A%C3%B1asco" title="R\xc3\xado Grande de A\xc3\xb1asco">R\xc3\xado Grande de A\xc3\xb1asco</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/R%C3%ADo_Culebrinas" class="mw-redirect" title="R\xc3\xado Culebrinas">R\xc3\xado Culebrinas</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/R%C3%ADo_Guajataca" class="mw-redirect" title="R\xc3\xado Guajataca">R\xc3\xado Guajataca</a><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>8<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li></ul>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Barrios">Barrios</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Barrios"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Like all municipalities of Puerto Rico, San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n is subdivided into <a href="/wiki/Barrios_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Barrios of Puerto Rico">barrios</a>. The municipal buildings, central square and large Catholic church are located in a barrio referred to as <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">"el pueblo"</i></span>.<sup id="cite_ref-Pico_1969_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pico_1969-9"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>9<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Law2015_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Law2015-10"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-US2010Census_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-US2010Census-11"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>11<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>12<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1184024115">.mw-parser-output .div-col{margin-top:0.3em;column-width:30em}.mw-parser-output .div-col-small{font-size:90%}.mw-parser-output .div-col-rules{column-rule:1px solid #aaa}.mw-parser-output .div-col dl,.mw-parser-output title="Sonador">Sonador</a></li></ol>\n</div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Sectors">Sectors</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Sectors"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1236090951">.mw-parser-output .hatnote{font-style:italic}.mw-parser-output div.hatnote{padding-left:1.6em;margin-bottom:0.5em}.mw-parser-output .hatnote i{font-style:normal}.mw-parser-output .hatnote+link+.hatnote{margin-top:-0.5em}@media print{body.ns-0 .mw-parser-output .hatnote{display:none!important}}</style><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Further information: <a href="/wiki/List_of_barrios_and_sectors_of_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico" title="List of barrios and sectors of San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n, Puerto Rico">List of barrios and sectors of San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n, Puerto Rico</a></div>\n<p>Barrios (which are like <a href="/wiki/Minor_civil_divisions" class="mw-redirect" title="Minor civil divisions">minor civil divisions</a>)<sup id="cite_ref-Barrio-Pueblo_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Barrio-Pueblo-13"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>13<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> are further subdivided into smaller areas called <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">sectores</i></span> (<i>sectors</i> in English). The types of <i>sectores</i> may vary, from normally <i>sector</i> to <i>urbanizaci\xc3\xb3n</i> to <i>reparto</i> to <i>barriada</i> to <i>residencial</i>, among others.<sup id="cite_ref-sectores_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sectores-14"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>14<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Special_Communities">Special Communities</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Special Communities"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Office_for_Socioeconomic_and_Community_Development" title="Puerto Rico Office for Socioeconomic and Community Development">Puerto Rico Office for Socioeconomic and Community Development</a></div>\n<p><span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">Comunidades Especiales de Puerto Rico</i></span> (Special Communities of Puerto Rico) are marginalized communities whose citizens are experiencing a certain amount of <a href="/wiki/Social_exclusion" title="Social exclusion">social exclusion</a>. A map shows these communities occur in nearly every municipality of the commonwealth. Of the 742 places that were on the list in 2014, the following barrios, communities, sectors, or neighborhoods were in San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n: Guaci\xc3\xb3 barrio, Boquer\xc3\xb3n, Chinto Rod\xc3\xb3n, Estalingrado, Paralelo 38, Parcelas Perchas II, Pueblo Nuevo, and Tablas Astilla.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>15<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Demographics">Demographics</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1224496135">.mw-parser-output .us-census-pop{border-spacing:1px;border:1px solid class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>21<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></td></tr>\n</tbody></table>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Tourism">Tourism</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Tourism"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Landmarks_and_places_of_interest">Landmarks and places of interest</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Landmarks and places of interest"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Established in 2016 is the <i>Veredas Sports Complex</i> in barrio <a href="/wiki/Guatemala,_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico" title="Guatemala, San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n, Puerto Rico">Guatemala</a>. The complex which consists of a modern <a href="/wiki/Skatepark" title="Skatepark">skate park</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Beach_volleyball" title="Beach volleyball">sand volleyball</a> court, a <a href="/wiki/Zipline" class="mw-redirect" title="Zipline">zipline</a> with four stations, a climbing and rappelling wall, an outdoor gym, a rope bridge, basketball and tennis courts, and walking paths, is set within an urban forest of about six thousand trees. <i>Hacienda La Fe</i>, an agriculture museum is located at the complex.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>23<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\nOther landmarks and places of interest in this municipality include:<sup id="cite_ref-Enciclopedia_PR_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Enciclopedia_PR-24"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>24<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:People_at_Gozalandia_Falls_in_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/People_at_Gozalandia_Falls_in_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg/220px-People_at_Gozalandia_Falls_in_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/People_at_Gozalandia_Falls_in_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg/330px-People_at_Gozalandia_Falls_in_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/People_at_Gozalandia_Falls_in_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg/440px-People_at_Gozalandia_Falls_in_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="853" /></a><figcaption>People at Gozalandia Falls in San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n</figcaption></figure>\n<p>The <i>Robles Waterfall</i> (located within the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Gozalandia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Gozalandia (page does not exist)">Gozalandia</a> waterfalls zone) \xe2\x80\x93 It is a favorite with the locals however, several deaths have occurred at Gozalandia, including tourists<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>25<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>26<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Iglesia_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n_M%C3%A1rtir" title="Iglesia San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n M\xc3\xa1rtir">Church of Saint Sebastian the Martyr</a> on the <a href="/wiki/National_Register_of_Historic_Places" title="National Register of Historic Places">US National Register of Historic Places</a>, is located in the <a href="/wiki/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n_barrio-pueblo" title="San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n barrio-pueblo">Pueblo of San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n</a>.\n</p><p>There is a <a href="/wiki/Farmers%27_market" title="Farmers&#39; market">farmer\'s market</a> held every Friday at the <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">Centro Agropecuario</i></span> that sells local agriculture as well as souvenirs, for tourists.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>27<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Museo_de_Historia_-_San_Sebastian_Puerto_Rico.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Museo_de_Historia_-_San_Sebastian_Puerto_Rico.jpg/330px-Museo_de_Historia_-_San_Sebastian_Puerto_Rico.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Museo_de_Historia_-_San_Sebastian_Puerto_Rico.jpg/440px-Museo_de_Historia_-_San_Sebastian_Puerto_Rico.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3500" data-file-height="2601" /></a><figcaption>The Casa de Do\xc3\xb1a Bisa Museum</figcaption></figure>\n<p>The <i>Casa de Do\xc3\xb1a Bisa Museum</i> located across from the main square in downtown features information on what life was like in the early 20th century.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>28<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Other sites include:\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Guajataca_Lake" title="Guajataca Lake">Guajataca Lake</a></li>\n<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luis_Aymat_Cardona_Coliseum&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Luis Aymat Cardona Coliseum (page does not exist)">Luis Aymat Cardona Coliseum</a></li>\n<li>Collazo Waterfall</li>\n<li>Hacienda El Jibarito</li>\n<li>Hacienda La Fe</li>\n<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Juan_Jose_%22Titi%22_Beniquez_Stadium&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Juan Jose &quot;Titi&quot; Beniquez Stadium (page does not exist)">Juan Jose "Titi" Beniquez Stadium</a></li>\n<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luis_Mu%C3%B1oz_Marin_Ground&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Luis Mu\xc3\xb1oz Marin Ground (page does not exist)">Luis Mu\xc3\xb1oz Marin Ground</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Guajataka_Scout_Reservation" title="Guajataka Scout Reservation">Guajataka Scout Reservation</a></li></ul>\n<div style="clear:both;" class=""></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Economy">Economy</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Economy"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Agriculture">Agriculture</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Agriculture"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Plaza_Agropecuaria_en_barrio_Guatemala,_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/Plaza_Agropecuaria_en_barrio_Guatemala%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg/220px-Plaza_Agropecuaria_en_barrio_Guatemala%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/Plaza_Agropecuaria_en_barrio_Guatemala%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg/330px-Plaza_Agropecuaria_en_barrio_Guatemala%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/Plaza_Agropecuaria_en_barrio_Guatemala%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg/440px-Plaza_Agropecuaria_en_barrio_Guatemala%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3557" data-file-height="2669" /></a><figcaption>Plaza Agropecuaria hosts a farmer\'s market on Fridays</figcaption></figure>\n<figure class="mw-default-size mw-halign-left" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Caf%C3%A9_El_Coqu%C3%AD_plant,_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Caf%C3%A9_El_Coqu%C3%AD_plant%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg/220px-Caf%C3%A9_El_Coqu%C3%AD_plant%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Caf%C3%A9_El_Coqu%C3%AD_plant%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg/330px-Caf%C3%A9_El_Coqu%C3%AD_plant%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Caf%C3%A9_El_Coqu%C3%AD_plant%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg/440px-Caf%C3%A9_El_Coqu%C3%AD_plant%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2941" data-file-height="2206" /></a><figcaption>Caf\xc3\xa9 El Coqu\xc3\xad plant in Perchas I</figcaption></figure>\n<p>San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n is a producer of coffee, fruits, and has dairy farms.<sup id="cite_ref-Enciclopedia_PR_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Enciclopedia_PR-24"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>24<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> There is a coffee production plant called El Coqu\xc3\xad located in <a href="/wiki/Perchas_1" title="Perchas 1">Perchas 1</a>, a barrio of San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n.<sup id="cite_ref-cafe-elcoqui_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cafe-elcoqui-29"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>29<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Government">Government</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Government"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Mayoralty_in_Puerto_Rico" class="mw-redirect" title="Mayoralty in Puerto Rico">Mayoralty in Puerto Rico</a></div>\n<p>Like all municipalities in <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a>, San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n is administered by a mayor. The current mayor is <a href="/wiki/Javier_Jim%C3%A9nez_(mayor)" title="Javier Jim\xc3\xa9nez (mayor)">Javier Jim\xc3\xa9nez</a>, from the <a href="/wiki/New_Progressive_Party_of_Puerto_Rico" class="mw-redirect" title="New Progressive Party of Puerto Rico">New Progressive Party</a> (PNP). Jim\xc3\xa9nez was elected at the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rican_general_election,_2004" class="mw-redirect" title="Puerto Rican general election, 2004">2004 general election</a>.\n</p><p>The city belongs to the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Senatorial_district_IV" class="mw-redirect" title="Puerto Rico Senatorial district IV">Puerto Rico Senatorial district IV</a>, which is represented by two Senators. In 2012, <a href="/wiki/Mar%C3%ADa_Teresa_Gonz%C3%A1lez" title="Mar\xc3\xada Teresa Gonz\xc3\xa1lez">Mar\xc3\xada Teresa Gonz\xc3\xa1lez</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gilberto_Rodr%C3%ADguez" title="Gilberto Rodr\xc3\xadguez">Gilberto Rodr\xc3\xadguez</a> were elected as District Senators.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>30<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Transportation">Transportation</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Transportation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>There are 30 bridges in San Sebastian.<sup id="cite_ref-bridge_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bridge-31"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>31<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>There is also an air strip in San Sebastian, near <a href="/wiki/Culebrinas_River" title="Culebrinas River">Culebrinas River</a>, which is visible on Google Earth.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>32<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The air strip is for the use of RC (radio-controlled) airplanes.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Culture">Culture</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Culture"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>In the town is a Fine Arts and Convention Center called <i>Centro de Convenciones y Bellas Artes</i>, which was in the last phase of its construction, as of February 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>33<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Festivals_and_events">Festivals and events</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Festivals and events"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Festival_de_la_Novilla,_Hacienda_La_Fe,_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico.png" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Festival_de_la_Novilla%2C_Hacienda_La_Fe%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.png/220px-Festival_de_la_Novilla%2C_Hacienda_La_Fe%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="132" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Festival_de_la_Novilla%2C_Hacienda_La_Fe%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.png/330px-Festival_de_la_Novilla%2C_Hacienda_La_Fe%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Festival_de_la_Novilla%2C_Hacienda_La_Fe%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.png/440px-Festival_de_la_Novilla%2C_Hacienda_La_Fe%2C_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.png 2x" data-file-width="968" data-file-height="580" /></a><figcaption>Heifer Festival and Hacienda La Fe mural in San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n in 2019</figcaption></figure>\n<p>San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n celebrates its <a href="/wiki/Fiestas_patronales_in_Puerto_Rico" title="Fiestas patronales in Puerto Rico">patron saint</a> festival in January. The <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">Fiestas Patronales de San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n</i></span> is a religious and cultural celebration that generally features parades, games, artisans, amusement rides, regional food, and live entertainment.<sup id="cite_ref-PR_Ency_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PR_Ency-7"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-J.D._2006_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-J.D._2006-34"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>34<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>The <i>San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n Heifer Festival</i> (Spanish: <a href="/wiki/Festival_de_la_Novilla" title="Festival de la Novilla">Festival de la Novilla</a>), celebrated every year on the first Sunday during the patron saint festival, is San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n\'s largest festival attracting thousands of people. The celebration features <a href="/wiki/List_of_amusement_rides" title="List of amusement rides">carnival rides</a>, the diverse <a href="/wiki/Music_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Music of Puerto Rico">music of Puerto Rico</a>, cows decorated with flowers, <a href="/wiki/Float_(parade)" title="Float (parade)">floats</a> and <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rican_cuisine" title="Puerto Rican cuisine">Puerto Rican cuisine</a>.  In January 2016, the town celebrated its 40th Heifer festival.<sup id="cite_ref-ENDI_Festival_2016_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ENDI_Festival_2016-35"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>35<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>36<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Other festivals and events celebrated in San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n include:\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Epiphany_(holiday)" title="Epiphany (holiday)">Three Kings Day</a> Festival \xe2\x80\x93 January</li>\n<li>Children\'s Festival \xe2\x80\x93 January</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Hammock" title="Hammock">Hammock</a> Festival \xe2\x80\x93 July</li>\n<li>Lighting of the <a href="/wiki/Christmas_tree" title="Christmas tree">Christmas tree</a> \xe2\x80\x93 November</li>\n<li>Cultural Evenings \xe2\x80\x93 third Thursday of the month</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Farmers%27_market" title="Farmers&#39; market">Farmers\' market</a> \xe2\x80\x93 every Friday</li></ul>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Sports">Sports</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Sports"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-default-size mw-halign-left" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Equipo_de_Volibol_Los_Caribes_de_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Equipo_de_Volibol_Los_Caribes_de_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg/220px-Equipo_de_Volibol_Los_Caribes_de_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="293" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Equipo_de_Volibol_Los_Caribes_de_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg/330px-Equipo_de_Volibol_Los_Caribes_de_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Equipo_de_Volibol_Los_Caribes_de_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg/440px-Equipo_de_Volibol_Los_Caribes_de_San_Sebasti%C3%A1n%2C_Puerto_Rico.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2736" data-file-height="3648" /></a><figcaption>Plaque honoring <i>Los Caribes</i></figcaption></figure>\n<p>The Luis Aymat Cardona Coliseum is where the <i>Los Caribes</i> volleyball team plays their games.\n</p><p>In amateur baseball or Double AA baseball, the city is represented by the <i>Patrulleros de San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n</i>, who play at the <i>Juan Jose "Titi" Beniquez</i> Stadium<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>37<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> and became champions of the Northwest area in 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>38<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Symbols">Symbols</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Symbols"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">municipio</i></span> has an official flag and coat of arms.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>39<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Flag">Flag</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Flag"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>It consists of a rectangular flag of the usual proportions, crossed by a white waved band that separates its red superior part from the inferior one, which is green.<sup id="cite_ref-LexJuris_(Leyes_y_Jurisprudencia)_de_Puerto_Rico_2020_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LexJuris_(Leyes_y_Jurisprudencia)_de_Puerto_Rico_2020-40"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>40<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Coat_of_arms">Coat of arms</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Coat of arms"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The Mountains: With silver-plated borders, represent the characteristic mountains under which the vegetable namesake of the town grow (<a href="/wiki/Cucumber" title="Cucumber">cucumbers</a>) \nThe Crown: Is the heraldic standard used to identify towns, villas and cities. The sugar cane and coffee ranches represent main agricultural products.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>41<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-LexJuris_(Leyes_y_Jurisprudencia)_de_Puerto_Rico_2020_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LexJuris_(Leyes_y_Jurisprudencia)_de_Puerto_Rico_2020-40"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>40<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Notable_people">Notable people</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Notable people"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Juan_Ben%C3%ADquez" title="Juan Ben\xc3\xadquez">Juan Ben\xc3\xadquez</a>, a former center fielder in Major League Baseball</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/%C3%81ngel_Mislan" title="\xc3\x81ngel Mislan">\xc3\x81ngel Mislan</a>, (1862\xe2\x80\x931911) musician and composer of danzas "Sara" and "Tu y Yo".</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Nilita_Vient%C3%B3s_Gast%C3%B3n" title="Nilita Vient\xc3\xb3s Gast\xc3\xb3n">Nilita Vient\xc3\xb3s Gast\xc3\xb3n</a>, (1903\xe2\x80\x931989) an educator, writer and journalist and the first woman president of the Puerto Rican Athenaeum.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Luis_Guti%C3%A9rrez" title="Luis Guti\xc3\xa9rrez">Luis V. Guti\xc3\xa9rrez</a>, first <a href="/wiki/Hispanic_and_Latino_Americans" title="Hispanic and Latino Americans">Latino</a> to be elected to <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">Congress</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Midwestern_United_States" title="Midwestern United States">Midwest</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Oscar_Lopez_Rivera" class="mw-redirect" title="Oscar Lopez Rivera">Oscar Lopez Rivera</a>, political prisoner.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Altemio_Sanchez" title="Altemio Sanchez">Altemio Sanchez</a>, Rapist and Serial Killer</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Luz_Odilia_Font" title="Luz Odilia Font">Luz Odilia Font</a>, Telenovela, theater and film actress</li>\n<li>Abimelec Torres, Contestant on <a href="/wiki/Idol_Puerto_Rico" title="Idol Puerto Rico">Idol Puerto Rico</a></li>\n<li>Estefania Soto Torres, <a href="/wiki/Miss_Universe_Puerto_Rico" title="Miss Universe Puerto Rico">Miss Universe Puerto Rico</a> 2020 (Placed Top 10 at <a href="/wiki/Miss_Universe_2020" title="Miss Universe 2020">Miss Universe 2020</a>)</li></ul>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Gallery">Gallery</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<ul class="gallery mw-gallery-packed">\n\t\t<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 202px">\n\t\t\t<div class="thumb" style="width: 200px;"><span
